b:T80e,MixAtlas = 可解释两轴分解 + 低成本不确定性搜索 + recipe 迁移。
(1) 两轴数据分解（domain decomposition）：
- 监督轴（task supervision axis）：把样本按“目标/监督形式”重组为 5 类 objective（文中列举 captioning、OCR、grounding、detection、VQA 等）。关键点是：不是把原始数据集当作黑盒，而是把同一数据集内不同 supervision 形式拆开，形成可控 portfolio 𝒫_task。
- 概念轴（image concept axis）：用视觉编码器（CLIP embedding）对图像做聚类，自动发现 10 个视觉域/概念簇，形成 𝒫_concept。该轴让配比能直接对“视觉分布覆盖”施加控制，而不是间接通过数据集名称。
- 低维可解释：论文强调“独立优化每个轴”，把原本高维的 dataset-mixture 变成两个低维 simplex 上的权重搜索，既降低搜索难度，也便于解释“哪个轴在提升哪个 benchmark”。
(2) 代理模型 + 高斯过程 surrogate 的不确定性感知搜索：
- 用小 proxy（Qwen2-0.5B）在少量候选 mixture 上进行 midtraining，得到下游基准分数 F(h)。
- 用 Gaussian Process 拟合 mixture→benchmark 的响应面，同时输出不确定性；用 GP-UCB acquisition 在探索/利用间权衡，选择下一批要训练的 mixture。相比随机/网格/一些 LLM-only mixture baseline 的直接迁移，GP-UCB 在同等 proxy 预算下更快找到高分配方。
- 支持两种目标：Generalist（加权平均 J(h)）与 Targeted（单一 benchmark 最大化）。
(3) Recipe transfer：把在 0.5B 上找到的权重迁移到 7B（Qwen2-7B、Qwen2.5-7B）做 full midtraining，验证其在更大规模下仍能带来更快收敛与更好下游；并提供“confidence-rated recipes”（由 GP 不确定性给出置信信息），便于工程落地时评估风险。
整体上，MixAtlas 的关键创新不是某个新 loss，而是把“多模态数据配比”工程问题形式化为可解释、可搜索、可迁移的优化问题，并给出一套可复用流程。c:T507,MixAtlas combines (i) interpretable decomposition, (ii) Bayesian optimization with proxies, and (iii) transfer:
1) Two-axis decomposition:
- Task supervision axis: re-buckets examples into 5 objective types (e.g., captioning, OCR, grounding, detection, VQA), forming a task portfolio. This breaks the “dataset as a black box” assumption and makes supervision signals directly controllable.
- Image concept axis: clusters images into 10 concept groups using CLIP embeddings, forming a concept portfolio that explicitly controls visual-domain coverage.
The mixture becomes a sampling distribution over each axis; the paper emphasizes optimizing axes independently to keep the search low-dimensional and interpretable.
2) Uncertainty-aware proxy search:
- Train a small proxy model (Qwen2-0.5B) on selected mixtures.
- Fit a Gaussian-process surrogate mapping mixture weights to benchmark scores, with predictive uncertainty.
- Use GP-UCB acquisition to choose the next mixtures, balancing exploration and exploitation under a fixed proxy budget.
3) Recipe transfer:
- Apply the discovered mixtures to full-scale midtraining (7B) and report both convergence and downstream improvements; provide confidence-rated recipes based on GP uncertainty to support practical deployment decisions.d:T4bf,They introduce ST-MoE (Semantic Trajectory MoE), a geometric routing MoE designed to vary routing topology while keeping other factors controlled.
- Geometric router: project token states from d_model to a low-dimensional d_space=64, L2-normalize, and route via cosine similarity to learned, normalized expert centroids; apply a fixed scale τ=30, softmax, then top-k with renormalization.
- Parameter-budget lever: across 8 layers, routing parameters drop from 8.39M (standard linear router nn.Linear(d_model→M)) to 1.57M (projection + centroids), a 5.3× reduction.
- Topology lever: support multi-hop re-routing—after each expert update, re-project and re-route—creating trajectories through expert space, enabling controlled comparisons across routing topologies/composition variants.
- Mechanistic analysis: multi-hop updates are largely collinear (avg cosine ≈ 0.805), behaving like convergent magnitude amplification rather than compositional expert reasoning; a single learnable scalar can match multi-hop performance.
- Equifinality quantification: cross-seed analyses show large above-random functional overlap despite different parameterizations, used as a quantitative signature of equifinality.e:T46c,From the full paper’s reported setup/results:
- Scale/data: 62 controlled experiments on WikiText-103; convergence study around 76–84M parameters, trained 50K steps on ~1.64B tokens.
- Topology equifinality: five cosine-routing topology variants converge to statistically equivalent PPL within a 1-PPL margin; TOST significance p<0.05 for all 10 pairwise comparisons; 15 runs over 3 seeds, PPL range ~33.93–34.72.
- Linear router reference: standard linear router reaches PPL ~32.76 but uses ~5.3× more routing parameters; the remaining gap is argued to be mostly capacity-driven.
- Ablation on routing space: routing directly in d_model=768 (no low-dim bottleneck) worsens PPL by ~3.1% and causes multi-hop to degenerate into repeated expert selection.
- Mechanism evidence: multi-hop collinearity (cos ~0.805); a single learnable scalar replicates multi-hop gains.
- Efficiency: zero-shot relative-norm halting saves ~25% MoE FLOPs at only +0.12% PPL at convergence.
- Architecture interaction: multi-hop prefers many small experts, while single-hop prefers fewer large experts, linked to centroid density in routing space.f:T574,Counterfactual Routing (CoR) is a training-free inference framework built on counterfactual (virtual ablation) analysis, with two coupled reallocations under a fixed compute budget.
- Offline causal analysis:
  1) Layer-wise perturbation/sensitivity analysis to identify knowledge-intensive layers vs syntax-dominant layers, motivated by prior findings that factual knowledge concentrates in certain layers.
  2) Expert-wise causal scoring via Counterfactual Expert Impact (CEI): for a given token/layer/expert, estimate how much the model’s prediction would change if that expert were counterfactually removed/replaced. CEI aims to capture causal necessity for factual correctness, unlike router gating probabilities which reflect correlation with training statistics.
- Online inference (compute-preserving redistribution):
  1) Layer-wise budget shifting: allocate more expert slots to knowledge-intensive layers and fewer to syntax-heavy layers, keeping the total number of activated experts constant.
  2) Expert-wise reranking: within a layer, “awaken” experts with high CEI but low gating (dormant specialists) by swapping them into the active set, replacing experts that are highly gated but low-CEI for the current prediction.
Overall, CoR acts as an inference-time routing override guided by counterfactual causality signals, without retraining routers/experts or using retrieval.10:T435,SpecGuard reframes SD around reasoning steps rather than individual tokens:
- Multi-candidate step drafting + self-consistency selection: the draft model samples multiple candidate steps; a selector picks the most semantically consistent/representative step to verify, reducing variance-induced derailment.
- Attention-Based Grounding Verification (ABGV): uses the model’s own attention matrices and attention rollout (layerwise multiplication of head-averaged attentions) to compute cumulative attribution from each generated token to the input and previously validated steps. A grounding score is computed per token; step grounding is the minimum token grounding within the step (a conservative criterion to catch a single hallucinated critical token).
- Log-probability verification: complements ABGV with target-model confidence on the drafted step.
- Ensemble verifier + adaptive fallback: combines grounding and logprob signals to decide whether to accept the drafted step or fall back to target generation, allocating compute adaptively without external reward models.11:T416,MemoSight turns two seemingly different techniques into one consistent autoregressive framework:
- Context compression via step-wise memory tokens (following LightThinker): after each reasoning step ends (delimiter token), append a fixed set of memory tokens that learn to summarize that step in their hidden states; at inference, discard the original step tokens and keep only memory tokens, shrinking KV-cache.
- MTP without extra heads: instead of d parallel prediction heads, it adopts a sequence-manipulation MTP (register/foresight tokens) where special tokens are assigned shifted/engineered position IDs so the same model can predict multiple future offsets in parallel.
- The key unification is “Special Tokens as Carriers” + “Position-Aware Alignment”: memory tokens are positioned/aligned to represent past steps, foresight tokens are positioned to represent future offsets. This avoids the performance drop observed with a naive combination, which likely creates misaligned positional semantics and competing training signals.12:T44e,ELMoE-3D unifies cache-based AR acceleration (low batch) and speculative decoding (high batch) on HB-based 3D-IC systems by leveraging two orthogonal elasticities:
- Expert elasticity: heavy-tailed routing implies a small set of hot experts dominate; expert throttling/hardware-aware selection reduces memory traffic.
- Bit elasticity: nested quantization enables on-demand precision scaling.
Key components:
1) Elastic Self-Speculative Decoding (Elastic-SD): cache MSB bit-slices of hot experts in residual HB memory to form a self-draft model with high alignment to the target while also reducing verification memory loads.
2) LSB-augmented bit-sliced architecture: repurpose sign-extension overhead in bit-sliced MAC as implicit LSB rounding, enabling bit-nested quantization without extra hardware cost.
3) Elasticity-aware execution engine: phase-aware scheduling across SD phases with mixed-precision execution spanning HB and external memory tiers.
Overall, it is a system that maps “parts of the MoE” into a draft+cache structure to raise arithmetic intensity and reduce bandwidth pressure.13:T6bb,The paper reframes inference as a compressed-sensing-style sparse recovery problem.

1) Measurements: instead of executing the full dense network, acquire a small number of cheap, randomized low-dimensional measurements (feature sketches / calibration probes) of prompt-conditioned and token-conditioned signals. The measurement operator is claimed to be task-conditioned to reflect prompt-specific internal usage patterns.

2) Support recovery: formulate routing/selection of structured compute units as recovering the support of a sparse latent vector under structured sparsity assumptions. The authors position classical CS tools (RIP, mutual incoherence) as a way to bound the number of measurements needed for reliable recovery.

3) Structured sparsity for hardware: constrain admissible supports to patterns that map to efficient GPU kernels (group sparsity over heads/channels/blocks), addressing the common gap where unstructured sparsity fails to yield wall-clock speedups.

4) Online, token-adaptive execution: unlike static pruning, the active support can vary across prompts and across decoding steps; measurement and recovery must be lightweight enough that overhead does not dominate.

5) Joint prompt + model reduction: prompt token removal and subnetwork selection are solved jointly, allowing the system to trade off sequence-length reduction vs executed-model reduction.

Differentiation: SparseGPT/Wanda focus on offline pruning (with/without activation awareness); ZipLM emphasizes inference-aware structured pruning but remains largely static; LLMLingua-style methods compress prompts only. This work claims a unified, principled inverse-problem formulation for dynamic routing plus prompt compression.14:T4a3,Two key components.
(1) Centroid replacement as a controlled probe: run K-means over token representations and replace each token vector with its nearest centroid, which collapses fine-grained geometry while keeping a coarse prototype. Apply the same operation separately to text tokens and vision tokens; the accuracy drop is interpreted as the model’s dependence on that modality’s learned structure.
(2) Text-centroid contrastive decoding: perform a second forward pass where text token structure is erased via centroid replacement, producing a reference distribution. Then decode contrastively against this reference to down-weight candidates that remain likely even when text structure is removed—effectively suppressing language-prior-driven outputs and encouraging reliance on visual evidence.
The paper strengthens the causal story with null controls (to show gains are specific to learned centroid geometry rather than generic noise) and a monotonic dose–response sweep. Additional localization via segment ablations and layer sweeps attributes the competition largely to answer-option token representations and shows the induced task sensitivity is stable across depth.15:T44f,TESSY (Teacher–Student Cooperation Data Synthesis) generates a single training sequence by interleaving teacher and student generation.

1) Token-type decomposition: define capability tokens (task-solving content such as code/numerical/critical operators) and style tokens (discourse markers, tone, connective text). The SFT objective is decomposed into capability loss and style loss; the authors argue that, for reasoning models, optimizing style loss toward a mismatched teacher can be hard and can harm capability learning.

2) Synthesis objective: sample capability-token distribution from the teacher while keeping style-token distribution close to the student.

3) Alternating generation with generate-then-rollback: the system generates segments, then selectively rolls back and lets the other model take over to enforce fine-grained division of labor (teacher for capability, student for style) within the same response.

4) Practical framing: this is a data-generation-time distribution-matching mechanism (a kind of mixed on-policy synthesis), rather than a training-time reweighting trick.16:T547,The framework explicitly decouples (1) task-specific gradient extraction and (2) conflict-aware gradient combination. Let g_r be the retain gradient (typically GD on retain data) and g_f be the forget gradient (from GA/NPO/SimNPO-style objectives). Instead of summing losses, the method synthesizes an update g that is constrained to be retention-friendly.

Two instantiations are provided:
- Adapted PCGrad: when g_f conflicts with g_r (negative inner product), project g_f to remove the component that opposes g_r, guaranteeing non-negative cosine similarity with g_r. Retention acts as the anchor; forgetting is only allowed within the feasible cone that does not harm retention.
- SAGO: strengthens the alignment guarantee beyond global cosine constraints by enforcing element-wise sign alignment between the synthesized update and g_r. This addresses cases where overall cosine similarity is non-negative but some coordinates still move against retention. The paper claims theoretical guarantees: both PCGrad and SAGO ensure non-negative cosine similarity with g_r, while SAGO achieves a strictly tighter alignment bound via constructive sign-constrained synthesis.

A major design point is modularity: the synthesizer can be applied on top of GA+GD, NPO+GD, SimNPO+GD, etc., making it an optimization primitive rather than a new unlearning loss.17:T4e1,The setup freezes a target LLM, extracts per-token internal activations across layers, concatenates them into features, and trains a linear probe producing token-level logits z_t. A causal sliding-window mean (e.g., M=16) smooths token noise. The main innovations are in how token/window logits are aggregated and regularized under exchange-level supervision:
1) Top-K supportive-window pooling: replaces softmax/hardmax-style spike-sensitive aggregation with an operator that effectively requires multiple windows to support the harmful prediction, reducing reliance on single-token cues.
2) Segment Variance Regularization (SegVar): penalizes dispersion in logit magnitudes across selected evidence windows, suppressing isolated spikes and encouraging stable, distributed evidence. It is applied selectively to benign exchanges to directly target false positives.
The paper also evaluates which internal streams to probe, finding attention/MLP outputs outperform the commonly used residual stream. Finally, it tests adversarial obfuscation via character-level ciphers and shows probes trained on base models transfer plug-and-play to cipher-tuned models, suggesting safety-relevant signals remain linearly readable despite surface transformations.18:T63b,Two aligned diagnostics on the same dataset/judges:
1) Transitivity / cycle analysis for pairwise judging:
- For each document x with n candidate system outputs S, the judge induces a directed tournament graph over S.
- A transitivity violation is defined as a directed 3-cycle (A≻B, B≻C, C≻A). They compute a per-document violation rate ρ(x) (normalized by the number of triples), and report not only the global mean ρ̄ but also the fraction of documents with any violation and the full distribution.
- To test whether cycles reflect systematic bias vs sparse noise, they compare multiple aggregation/ranking methods (WinRate, Bradley–Terry, Schulze) and “repair” methods based on Minimum Feedback Arc Set (MFAS) solved exactly via ILP or approximated via Copeland, then measure agreement with human rankings (Kendall’s τ).
2) Split conformal prediction sets for direct Likert scoring:
- The judge outputs ŷ∈{1..5}; the target y* is the rounded mean human score.
- Using calibration residuals |ŷ−y*| as nonconformity scores, they compute an empirical quantile threshold to build prediction sets C(x) with finite-sample, distribution-free marginal coverage ≥1−α.
- The key operational metric is set width w(x)=|C(x)| (1 to 5), evaluated as a predictor of actual judge-human error via Spearman correlation, and as a document-difficulty signal via inter-judge width agreement.
The main methodological contribution is shifting from aggregate correlations to distributional, instance-level diagnostics, and validating that “cycle fixing” does not rescue reliability.19:T50e,Setup: SummEval with four criteria (coherence, consistency, fluency, relevance). For cost, they subsample to 30 documents × 8 systems. Four instruction-tuned judges via OpenRouter: GPT-4o-mini, LLaMA-3.1-70B-Instruct, Qwen-2.5-72B-Instruct, and Mistral-Small-3.1-24B-Instruct. Pairwise comparisons are repeated k=3 times.
Key findings reported in the paper:
- Global cycle rates look small (mean ρ̄ = 0.8%–4.1%), yet 33%–67% of documents exhibit at least one directed 3-cycle; the worst-case document reaches ρ(x)=30.4% for Mistral-Small.
- MFAS-based ranking repair does not improve Kendall’s τ vs human rankings, suggesting cycles behave like sparse noise rather than correctable directional bias.
- Conformal prediction sets achieve the intended coverage behavior, and set width strongly predicts judge-human disagreement: pooled across 1,918 observations, Spearman rs = +0.576 with p < 1e−100.
- Width agreement across different judges on the same documents is moderate (reported average correlations around 0.32–0.38 for several criteria), supporting the interpretation that width captures inherent document difficulty.
- Both diagnostics indicate criterion matters more than judge identity; coherence/relevance are more trustworthy than fluency/consistency in this setting.1a:T410,MARS^2 (Multi-Agent Reinforced Tree-Search Scaling) unifies multi-agent RL and tree search by treating the search tree as a learnable multi-agent environment:
- Multiple independently-optimized agents jointly expand a shared search tree, so the tree is no longer governed by a single policy distribution.
- Collaboration is embedded into the search dynamics (branching, selection, backtracking, budget usage), not as an after-the-fact ensemble.
- A path-level group advantage is introduced for credit assignment over entire root-to-node (or root-to-leaf) trajectories, aggregating multi-agent contributions to reduce variance and mitigate non-stationarity from concurrent policy updates.
- Tree-consistent reward shaping propagates outcome feedback in a way consistent with tree structure, stabilizing learning signals across depths/branches.
Overall, it reframes “search-augmented RL” from a static sampling add-on into a closed-loop training environment where multi-policy diversity is the key lever for sustained exploration scaling.1b:T408,The paper is primarily benchmark engineering and a scalable construction pipeline:
- Task formulation: given a bug report and the full repository, an agent can read/edit files and run shell commands to produce a patch; correctness is checked by the project’s native simulation/regression inside a container (execution-grounded).
- Data sourcing: 417 instances mined from real merged bug-fix PRs linked to issues across six major open-source hardware projects (Verilog/SystemVerilog + Chisel).
- Reproducibility pipeline: multi-stage filtering to isolate genuine bug fixes, then per-instance containerization to standardize heterogeneous hardware build/verification flows (a key challenge vs software due to toolchain diversity and missing automated tests).
- Evaluation protocol: multiple LLMs (proprietary + open) and multiple agent frameworks are run across all repos; results are broken down by repository scope/bug types and analyzed via recurring failure modes (localization, hardware semantics, cross-artifact coordination).1c:T4ad,R2A (Route to Rome Attack) follows a surrogate-then-optimize paradigm tailored to routers:
1) Hybrid ensemble surrogate router: since real-world routers vary widely (embedding-based, classifier-based, LLM-based loss/quality predictors, etc.) and the target router is unknown, R2A builds an ensemble surrogate Rs combining multiple open-source routing mechanisms plus lightweight trainable routers. Using limited black-box queries to the target Rt (input → chosen model), it fits Rs to mimic Rt’s decision boundary. The key bet is architectural diversity: an ensemble better matches an unknown router under low sample budgets.
2) Ensemble-aware adversarial suffix optimization: with Rs in hand, R2A optimizes a discrete suffix appended to arbitrary queries to maximize the chance of being routed to the expensive model set. The optimization is adapted to aggregate signals across the ensemble components to improve transfer to Rt, producing a universal trigger-like suffix that generalizes across queries and routers.
Overall, the novelty is less about a new gradient estimator and more about making universal suffix attacks work in a decision-only router setting via a robust surrogate design.1d:T446,MindDR combines a 3-agent inference architecture with a 4-phase training pipeline.
- Inference decomposition: Planning Agent (task planning), DeepSearch Agent (multi-step retrieval/navigation), Report Agent (conflict resolution + structured report writing). A shared memory substrate and an Extended Chain-of-Thought (XoT) mechanism coordinate collaboration, aiming to parallelize search and isolate contexts to avoid ultra-long single-context inference.
- Training pipeline:
(i) SFT cold start for instruction following and tool use;
(ii) Search-RL for the DeepSearch Agent with step-level credit assignment to optimize long-horizon search efficiency and reduce redundant token/tool usage;
(iii) Report-RL using RACE rubrics and format-based reward shaping to improve conflict resolution and long-form quality;
(iv) Preference alignment with human feedback signals to calibrate reports to user expectations.
- Evaluation: benchmarks include BrowseComp(-ZH), GAIA, xbench-DS, DeepResearch Bench, plus the new MindDR Bench; metrics cover search process, content quality, and presentation 要解决的是：如何在可解释、可迁移、低成本的前提下，为特定 benchmark 目标（或通用平均目标）自动优化多模态 midtraining 数据配比。","importance":"这是偏“数据科学/配比优化”的预训练关键问题，贡献量级较大：\n- 把多模态混合从“按数据集调权”推进到“按监督类型×视觉概念”两轴可控空间，显著提升可解释性与可操作性（利于数据迭代与定向补数）。\n- 用不确定性感知的代理模型搜索（proxy + GP surrogate + UCB）把 mixture 优化从昂贵的网格/随机试验变成样本效率更高的贝叶斯优化流程，直接服务于 scaling 时代的训练决策。\n- 证明 recipe 可从 0.5B proxy 迁移到 7B 级 midtraining，并带来收敛加速（最多 2× steps 减少）与下游提升（跨 10 个基准平均提升 MixAtlas addresses how to derive benchmark-targeted, interpretable, and compute-efficient mixture recipes that can be searched with small proxy models and transferred to large-scale midtraining.","importance":"A substantial data-centric contribution for foundation-model training:\n- Replaces opaque dataset-level weighting with an interpretable two-axis control space (visual LLM 专家集合，避免传统范式中每扩展一次能力就要人工启动新训练、固定数据/奖励、最终只产出单一模型的局限。","importance":"对预训练/持续学习研究的启发在于：把“数据生成（任务）—模型更新（参数）—评测/选择（覆盖度）”做成闭环的开放式共进化系统，强调能力多样性与群体覆盖（collective coverage）而非单模型单指标最优。这为持续学习、合成数据驱动的能力扩展、以及“多模型集群替代单一巨模”的 scaling 路线提供了方法论参考。但需要注意：该工作更像一种模型开发/搜索范式（evolution + merging + synthetic tasks），而非提出新的语言建模目标或可直接迁移到大规模预训练的优化机制。","technical_approach":"AC/DC（Assessment Coevolving w/ Diverse Capabilities）核心由两条共进化链路组成：\n1) 模型侧：用进化式模型合并（基于 EvoMerge / CMA-ES 思路）在现有 LLM 之间做 crossover/merge 产生新个体，而不是从零训练；通过选择机制保留在不同任务维度上表现互补的模型，形成“专家档案库（archive）”。\n2) 任务侧：通过合成数据生成不断产生新的自然语言任务/评测，作为对模型群体的动态压力（open-endedness），并设置最小质量门槛（minimal criteria）避免退化。\n3) 评估与选择：引入 Coverage 指标衡量“模型集合”对任务集合的覆盖广度，用质量-多样性（QD）原则驱动选择，而非显式对固定 benchmark 过拟合。\n整体流程是：任务生成→评测模型群体→基于覆盖/质量选择父代→合并产生子代→更新任务与模型档案库，循环迭代。","experiments":"论文报告的主结论包括：\n- 共进化迭代越多，模型群体在测试时（对合成任务 OOD 的标准 LLM 具体是什么）；\n  (b) archive 如何维护、子集如何选取做 coverage 最大化；\n  (c) OOD benchmark 评测协议（是否有数据泄漏控制、是否与合成任务分布重叠）。\n- 如果时间有限：优先看 coverage 指标与选择策略的消融，其次看“同等总参数预算下，群体 vs 单模型”的对比。","authors_note":""},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"Designing an open-ended, single-run framework that coevolves (1) a population of LLMs and (2) a continually shifting set of natural-language tasks, so that the system can autonomously discover novel capabilities and diverse experts—without repeatedly launching manual training runs on static datasets or reward functions.","importance":"The paper is most relevant as a methodology for continual capability expansion driven by a closed loop of synthetic task generation, population-level selection, and low-cost model updates via merging. It reframes scaling from “one bigger model” to “a collective of smaller specialists” optimized for coverage and diversity. For pretraining researchers, the key takeaway is the system-level recipe for open-ended data/task curricula and population-based capability discovery, though it is less about new language modeling objectives or core optimizer/scaling-law advances.","technical_approach":"AC/DC (Assessment Coevolving with Diverse Capabilities) couples two evolutionary processes:\n- Model coevolution: new candidate LLMs are produced via evolutionary model merging (building on EvoMerge/CMA-ES-style search), using operations like crossover/merging between parent models rather than training from scratch.\n- Task coevolution: new synthetic natural-language tasks are generated continuously, with minimal quality criteria to prevent collapse, creating an ever-changing evaluation environment.\n- Selection objective: instead of optimizing a fixed benchmark, AC/DC uses a Coverage metric for a model set (population) and quality-diversity principles to maintain an archive of complementary experts.\nThe loop iterates: generate tasks → evaluate population → select parents by coverage/quality → merge to create offspring → update archives of tasks and models.","experiments":"Reported findings include: more coevolution iterations improve population test-time performance; a fixed-size subset of evolved models achieves broader benchmark coverage than larger single models from the same family and than the initial seed population; and at least one evolved model surpasses the best seed on MMLU (referenced around Fig. 1). Existing approaches rely on heuristic strategies to align mismatched vocabularies, introducing considerable complexity. In this paper, we propose a simple but effective baseline called Byte-Level Distillation (BLD) which enables CTD by operating at a common interface across tokenizers: the byte level. Quality","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p3","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"llm_pretrain","cover_url":"/covers/2604_14419.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.AI"],"summary":{"core_problem":"在稀疏 MoE 语言模型中，社区长期默认“更复杂的路由拓扑（multi-hop、层级、链式组合等）会带来更好的语言建模质量”。本文基于大量受控对照实验，直接检验这一假设：在训练到收敛的条件下，路由拓扑本身是否决定（或显著影响）最终困惑度；以及若存在差异，差异主要来自“路由机制/拓扑”还是“路由容量（router 参数/表示容量）”。","importance":"对预训练研究的价值主要在于：\n1) 纠偏 MoE 研究的优化方向：在固定训练预算与模型规模下，最终 PPL 的主要瓶颈更可能来自 router capacity（以及其可表达的判别边界/分配粒度），而不是路由拓扑花样；这会影响 MoE 预训练的架构搜索与参数预算分配（router vs experts）。\n2) 提供“等终性（equifinality）”的实证证据：不同路由拓扑/参数化可收敛到统计等价的语言建模质量，提示我们在 MoE 训练动态中存在大量函数等价解；这对理解 MoE 的可辨识性、训练不确定性、以及 scaling 实验的方差控制有启发。\n3) 工程层面给出可用的低成本路由替代：用低维几何路由（cosine + centroid）在显著减少路由参数的同时保持接近的收敛性能，并进一步用“相对范数 halting”在几乎不损质量的情况下减少 MoE FLOPs，属于“预训练架构/训练效率”交叉点的可落地结论。","technical_approach":"核心方法是构建并系统对比一种几何路由 MoE：ST-MoE（Semantic Trajectory MoE）。\n- 路由参数化：将 token 表示 h∈R^{d_model} 通过线性投影到低维 d_space（文中固定 64），并做 L2 归一化；每个 expert i 维护一个同维度、L2 归一化的可学习 centroid c_i。路由分数为 cosine(h_proj, c_i) 乘以固定温度/尺度 τ=30，再 softmax 后做 top-k 选择并重归一化权重。与标准线性 router（nn.Linear(d_model→M)）相比，路由参数从 8 层合计 8.39M 降到 1.57M（约 -80%，5.3× 更少）。\n- 拓扑/组合：支持 multi-hop rerouting（token 经过一个 expert 更新后再次投影并重新路由，形成“轨迹”），从而可实现多跳、链式、层级等“拓扑变化”的对照。\n- 关键对照思想：在同一训练设置下做大量受控实验，区分三类因素：路由容量（参数/维度/可分性）、路由机制（线性 vs cosine/几何）、路由拓扑（single-hop vs multi-hop/trajectory 变体）。论文给出一个经验排序：routing capacity >> routing mechanism >> routing topology≈composition method >> expert capacity。\n- 机制解释：作者在全文中不仅报告结果，还分析 multi-hop 的“表面组合性”可能是幻觉：多跳更新在表示空间中高度共线（平均 cos≈0.805），更像是沿同一方向做幅度放大/收敛式迭代，而非真正的“组合推理/分工协作”；因此用一个可学习标量就能复现 multi-hop 的收益。\n- 等终性度量：跨随机种子/不同参数化下，出现“功能重叠远高于随机”的现象（文中描述为 500× above-random functional overlap），作为 equifinality 的定量签名。","experiments":"实验设置与关键数字（来自全文描述）：\n- 规模与数据：主要在 WikiText-103 上做 62 个受控实验；收敛研究使用约 76–84M 参数模型，训练 50K steps，总计约 1.64B tokens。\n- 结论 1（拓扑等价）：五种 cosine-routing 拓扑/变体在收敛后 PPL 统计等价，差异在 1 PPL 以内；作者用 TOST（Two One-Sided Tests）检验，10 组两两比较均 p<0.05；15 次运行（3 seeds），PPL 范围约 33.93–34.72。\n- 结论 2（与线性 router 的差距主要来自容量）：标准线性 router 的 PPL≈32.76，但其路由参数约为几何路由的 5.3×；作者主张差距“主要由 routing capacity 解释”，而非拓扑。\n- 关键消融：若不做低维瓶颈、直接在 d_model=768 空间做路由，PPL 下降（变差）约 3.1%，且 multi-hop 退化为重复选择同一 expert（说明低维几何空间对路由判别/稳定性很关键）。\n- 机制实验：multi-hop 更新向量共线性（cos≈0.805）；用单一可学习标量可复现 multi-hop 性能（支持“幅度放大而非组合”的解释）。\n- 计算节省：提出 zero-shot relative-norm halting，在收敛模型上可节省约 25% MoE FLOPs，PPL 仅 +0.12%（质量损失极小）。\n- 结构观察：multi-hop 更偏好“更多更小的 experts”，single-hop 更偏好“更少更大的 experts”，作者将其归因于路由空间中 centroid 密度与覆盖方式（属于架构-路由耦合的经验规律）。","reading_guide":"泛读建议（但这篇其实接近 must-read 的方法论价值）：\n1) 先看 Section 4.3（routing topology equifinality）与对应表格/统计检验：这是全文最关键的因果结论来源，注意作者如何控制变量、如何做 TOST、以及“1-PPL margin”的判定口径。\n2) 再看 dualism）：如果你关心预训练效率/路由预算分配，这两节给出可直接迁移到更大规模 MoE 的启发。\n预计阅读时间：30–45 分钟（若要复现实验设计/统计检验细节，建议 1–2 小时）。","authors_note":""},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"MoE research often assumes that increasingly sophisticated routing topologies (multi-hop trajectories, hierarchical gating, chain-of-experts composition) improve language modeling quality. This paper tests that assumption at convergence: does routing topology actually determine final perplexity, or are observed gains mostly explained by router capacity (parameter/representation budget) rather than topology/mechanism?","importance":"Key takeaways for foundation-model pretraining:\n1) Reallocating attention in MoE design: under controlled settings, router capacity dominates, while routing topology is largely quality-neutral at convergence. 在长尾知识/罕见实体查询上更易幻觉的一个结构性原因：静态 Top-k 路由在训练分布主导下偏好高频“相关性”模式，导致承载长尾事实的“专家型 experts”在特定上下文中 gating 分数偏低而被长期不激活（dormant），模型“存了知识但路由没召回”，从而在推理时生成看似合理但错误的内容。论文要解决的是：在不改训练、不增加总激活专家数（compute-preserving）的前提下，推理阶段如何动态唤醒这些对事实正确性具有因果贡献但被路由忽略的专家。","importance":"对预训练/大模型研究的启发主要在 MoE 机制层面而非训练配方：它把 MoE 幻觉的一部分归因于“路由的相关-因果错配”，并给出一个训练外（training-free）的因果度量来重分配专家预算。对基座预训练的直接影响有限（不改变预训练目标/数据/优化），但对 MoE 作为 scaling 路线的可靠性很关键：提示我们在 MoE scaling 时，路由学习到的统计偏好可能系统性压制长尾知识专家；未来可能需要在预训练阶段引入因果/反事实路由正则、长尾感知的路由学习或分层预算机制。","technical_approach":"提出 Counterfactual Routing (CoR)，核心是用“反事实/虚拟消融”估计专家对当前预测的因果必要性，并据此在层级与专家级两条轴上做计算量守恒的专家预算重分配。\n1) 离线因果分析（offline）：\n- 层级视角：基于“知识集中在特定层”的经验（如 MEMIT/知识定位相关工作），对各层做扰动/敏感性分析，识别 knowledge-intensive layers 与 syntax-dominant layers。\n- 专家视角：定义 Counterfactual Expert Impact (CEI)。直观上是对某个 token、某层、某 expert，比较“正常激活该 expert”与“反事实地移除/替换该 expert（virtual ablation）”时模型输出（尤其是与事实相关的预测）变化幅度，从而得到该 expert 的因果贡献分数。CEI 与 router gating score 的关键区别：gating score 是相关性（训练统计偏好），CEI 试图刻画对当前正确预测的因果必要性。\n2) 在线推理重路由（online inference）：\n- 计算量守恒：总激活专家数不变，只在层间/专家间重新分配。\n- 层间重分配：对知识密集层动态“扩充”每 token 的 expert budget，同时在语法主导层相应“缩减”，保持总预算不变。\n- 专家内重分配：在某层内，用 CEI 识别“高 CEI 但低 gating”的 dormant specialists，并将其纳入激活集合，替换掉部分“高 gating 但低 CEI”的 generalists。\n整体上，CoR 是一个推理期的因果引导路由器外插层，不需要再训练 router/experts，也不依赖外部检索。","experiments":"全文给出的关键信息（基于你提供的正文片段）包括：\n- 模型：Qwen-3-30B-A3B（每 token 激活约 gating，导致事实错误。\n注：你提供的全文内容在实验细节处被截断，未包含具体基准名称、指标定义（如 factuality/accuracy/faithfulness）、各模型分项数字、消融（仅层间重分配 vs 仅 CEI vs 两者结合）、以及 CEI 计算开销/延迟影响等；这些需要在论文实验章节与附录中核对。","reading_guide":"泛读建议（skim，约 20-35 绑定）、以及“compute-preserving”的预算约束是如何在层间/层内同时满足的。\n- 实验部分建议快速定位：\n  1) 3.1% 提升对应哪些数据集/指标；\n  2) 消融：仅层预算重分配、仅 CEI、二者结合；\n  3) 额外开销：CEI 是否需要多次前向/局部重算、对吞吐/延迟影响；\n  4) 失败案例：是否会伤害流畅性/语法、或在非长尾问题上退化。\n- long-tail factual queries partly due to a structural routing issue: static Top-k routers are trained under frequency-dominated corpora and thus prefer high-frequency correlation patterns. As a result, fact-bearing “specialist” experts can be causally important yet receive low gating scores in the current context and remain inactive (dormant). The paper targets an inference-time, training-free way to “recall” such dormant experts while keeping the total activated-expert budget unchanged (compute-preserving).","importance":"This is more of a MoE mechanism/reliability contribution than a pretraining recipe contribution. Its key value for foundation-model researchers is the framing of a correlation–causality mismatch in MoE routing as a hallucination driver, plus a concrete counterfactual metric to reallocate expert budget at inference. It suggests that MoE scaling may systematically suppress long-tail knowledge experts unless routing is made long-tail/causality-aware during pretraining (e.g., counterfactual routing regularization, layer-wise budget learning, or long-tail-aware router objectives).","technical_approach":"$f","experiments":"From the provided full-text excerpt: evaluated on Qwen-3-30B-A3B (activating ~3B out of 30B per token), DeepSeek-V2-Lite, and GPT-OSS-20B. prompts. Existing compression methods mostly operate in token space (dropping/summarizing or soft prompts) and overlook redundancy in the latent embedding space. The goal is to compress every contiguous block of K input tokens into a single embedding—reducing effective prompt length—while keeping generation in the original vocabulary.","importance":"This is primarily an efficiency/serving-side technique rather than a new pretraining paradigm, but it is relevant to foundation-model research because it reframes compression as an embedding-space problem and avoids vocabulary expansion. It suggests a potential future direction where models are trained (or continually adapted) to be robust to compressed latent representations, complementing tokenizer-level innovations.","technical_approach":"K-Token Merging compresses the input only: for an input of length KN (pad to multiple of K), it looks up the original embeddings and feeds each K-embedding block into a lightweight encoder f (an MLP, ~50MB) to produce one compressed embedding. The compressed sequence is then processed by an LLM adapted with LoRA. During generation, the model outputs normal vocabulary tokens; newly generated tokens are appended uncompressed to a mixed compressed/uncompressed prefix.\nTraining jointly optimizes the encoder and LoRA, but the loss is computed only on uncompressed (generated) token positions, sidestepping the need to reconstruct the compressed input tokens. Reasoning","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p2","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"efficient","cover_url":"/covers/2604_15244.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"在多步推理场景中，传统 speculative decoding 以“token”为验证粒度，容易让早期错误在后续步骤中扩散；同时其“严格无偏接受”机制会拒绝语义上正确但在 target model 下概率偏低的草稿，导致算力浪费与加速收益受限。论文要解决的是：不依赖外部 verifier/reward model 的前提下，如何在保持推理正确率的同时，让 SD 在“步骤级”更稳健、更高效。","importance":"对基座预训练本身不是直接贡献，但对“推理时计算分配/解码-验证机制”有启发：1) 把验证粒度从 token 提升到 step，有助于抑制 reasoning error propagation；2) 用模型内部信号（attention 归因 + logprob 置信）替代外部 PRM，降低系统复杂度与额外延迟；3) 提供一种可解释的、与模型结构强绑定的 verifier 设计思路（attention rollout grounding），可能反向影响后续预训练/中训练阶段对“可验证性/可归因性”的建模目标设计。","technical_approach":"SpecGuard 是一个“step-level speculative decoding”框架，核心由三块组成：\n(1) Step 级候选生成 + 自一致性选择（self-consistency selector）：每个推理步骤由 draft model 采样多个候选 step（不是逐 token 单一路径），然后选择语义最一致/最具代表性的 step 作为待验证对象。论文强调该选择器用于降低 draft 随机性带来的偏航，从而减少后续验证失败与回退。\n(2) 模型内部的 Attention-Based Grounding Verification (ABGV)：利用 target/draft（文中表述为“model itself”）的注意力矩阵做 attention rollout。对每个输出 token 计算其对输入 tokens（包含原始问题与已验证历史步骤）的累计归因分布 R_{y_{i,t}}，并定义 grounding score 衡量该 token 是否“扎根于输入/历史”。step 级分数采用更严格的 min-over-tokens（G_min-step），即一步里最不 grounded 的 token 决定该步是否可信，用于防止某个关键 token 的幻觉破坏整步正确性。\n(3) Log-probability-based verification：用 target model 对 draft step 的 token-level logprob/置信度做补充验证，弥补 attention grounding 可能“看起来相关但其实错”的情况。\n(4) Ensemble verifier + 自适应算力分配：将 ABGV 与 logprob 信号集成为轻量 verifier，决定：接受 draft step、拒绝并回退到 target 生成，或触发更多计算（例如重新采样/更严格验证）。整体目标是在不引入外部 PRM 的情况下，减少无效验证与错误传播。","experiments":"从全文可见的关键信息：\n- 任务类型：多步推理（数学/知识密集等）基准；对比对象包含标准 SD 以及带外部 reward/verifier 的变体（文中提到 RSD）。\n- 主要结论：在多种推理基准上，相比 SOTA 方法，SpecGuard 在降低延迟的同时提升准确率；论文声称“准确率最高提升 3.6%，延迟降低约 <m1>…<ml>，并以触发 token <b> 开启下一步。训练时这些 memory tokens 通过注意力聚合该 step 的语义；推理时一旦 memory tokens 计算完成，就丢弃该 step 的原始 reasoning tokens，仅保留 memory tokens 作为“可缓存的压缩历史”，从而减少 KV-cache。\n2) 多 token 预测（Foresight 统一点（MemoSight）：关键不是简单把两者拼接，而是提出“Special Tokens as Carriers + Position-Aware Alignment”。即：memory tokens 对齐过去（压缩历史），foresight tokens 对齐未来（并行预测），并为两类 token 设计各自的 position layout，避免 naive 组合时出现训练目标互相干扰、位置对齐混乱导致性能下降的问题。整体保持架构不变，通过 token 类型与位置布局把两种训练信号放到同一自回归框架里。","experiments":"全文给出的核心结论是：在 4 个推理基准上，MemoSight 相比不压缩/或单独方法，在“准确率基本不降（甚至可与未压缩模型持平）”的同时，将 KV-cache 占用最多降低 66%，端到端推理加速最高 accuracy, by jointly addressing (i) the linear KV-cache growth with generated tokens and (ii) the incompatibility between context-compression training (typically post-training with memory tokens) and Inference-Aware Structured Reduction for Large Language Models","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p3","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"efficient","cover_url":"/covers/2604_14156.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"如何把“模型压缩/结构化剪枝”和“prompt 压缩”从彼此割裂的离线手段，统一成一种面向推理时动态变化的“稀疏支持集恢复”问题：在给定 prompt 与每个 decoding step 下，快速识别真正需要执行的结构化子网络（block/head/channel/neuron 等）以及需要保留的输入 token，从而在不显著损伤生成质量的前提下获得真实端到端加速。","importance":"对基座预训练研究的直接影响有限（更偏推理侧的动态稀疏执行/系统），但提供了一个值得借鉴的“把推理路径视为可恢复的稀疏结构”的建模视角：1）把 token/step 条件化的激活路径显式化，有助于理解与利用 LLM 的条件计算特性；2）把结构化稀疏约束与硬件可执行 kernel 对齐，强调“可测量—可恢复—可编译”的闭环；3）若该框架能稳定落地，可能反向影响预训练阶段（例如引入路由可恢复性正则、或为动态子网执行而预训练）。但就本文给出的内容来看，更像方法论/框架性主张，预训练层面的可复用结论需要更多实证支撑。","technical_approach":"核心思想是把一次推理（prompt 条件 + token 条件）下“哪些结构单元需要被激活”视为一个结构化稀疏向量的支持集（support）恢复问题，并用 compressed sensing 的测量—恢复范式来做在线选择。\n\n1）测量（Measurements）：不直接全量跑 dense 网络，而是对 prompt-conditioned / token-conditioned 的特征做低成本随机测量/特征 sketch/校准 probe，得到低维观测。论文强调测量算子应当 task-conditioned，以匹配不同 prompt 诱发的不同内部使用模式。\n\n2）恢复（Sparse recovery）：将“选择哪些 block/head/channel/neuron 执行”形式化为稀疏逆问题，在结构化稀疏假设下恢复支持集；并声称可用 RIP、互不相干等经典 compressed sensing 工具给出测量数需求的上界（更偏理论定位）。\n\n3）结构化约束（Structured sparsity）：支持集不允许任意稀疏，而限制为能映射到 GPU 等硬件高效 kernel 的结构（例如按 head/通道/块的成组稀疏），以避免 SparseGPT 类非结构稀疏“有 sparsity 无 speedup”的问题。\n\n4）在线/逐 token 自适应（Token-adaptive execution）：与静态剪枝不同，支持集可随 prompt 变化、也可随生成步变化；强调测量与恢复必须足够便宜，否则测量开销会抵消收益。\n\n5）与 prompt 压缩联合（Joint prompt+model reduction）：把“删 token”与“删计算单元”放到同一恢复目标中，系统在不同情形下自动权衡：缩短序列 vs 缩小执行子网 vs 两者同时。\n\n与既有工作差异：SparseGPT/Wanda 主要是离线重要性估计与一次性剪枝；ZipLM 强调结构化与推理可加速但仍偏静态；LLMLingua/LongLLMLingua Cost of Language: Centroid Erasure Exposes and Exploits Modal Competition in Multimodal Language Models","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p2","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"multimodal","cover_url":"/covers/2604_14363.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL","cs.AI","cs.CV"],"summary":{"core_problem":"多模态语言模型在“需要真实视觉感知”的任务上表现显著落后，其根因之一是语言表征在融合与解码中系统性压制视觉证据（modal competition / modal imbalance）。论文要解决的是：如何用一种训练无关、可解释、可量化的前向探针来诊断这种不平衡，并进一步在不改权重的前提下做推理期纠偏以提升视觉感知类任务准确率。","importance":"对基座/预训练研究的价值主要在“诊断与推理期干预”而非提出新的预训练范式：1）提供了一个可复用的、训练无关的 modal dependence 标量度量（用结构擦除带来的性能损失来衡量模态贡献），可作为多模态预训练/后训练配方的审计工具；2）揭示跨架构家族的普遍不对称：擦除文本结构的代价远高于擦除视觉结构，支持“语言先验主导”是系统性问题；3）提出一种两次前向的对比解码策略，在不训练的情况下在部分视觉感知任务上带来可观增益，提示多模态模型的失败模式部分来自解码阶段对语言流形的过度依赖。对预训练的直接启发是：需要在训练目标、token/表示对齐、以及解码/对齐阶段显式抑制语言先验对视觉证据的吞噬。","technical_approach":"核心方法由两部分组成。\n(1) Centroid replacement（质心替换）作为受控“结构擦除”探针：对某一模态的 token 表示做 K-means 聚类，将每个 token 向量替换为其最近质心，从而在尽量保持一阶统计/幅值的同时，擦除细粒度几何结构（作者将其视为对 learned representation geometry 的定向破坏）。分别对 text tokens 与 vision tokens 做该替换，比较任务准确率下降幅度，作为该模态结构对最终预测的依赖度。\n(2) Text centroid contrastive decoding（文本质心对比解码）：对同一输入做两次前向：一次原始模型输出；一次对文本 token 做 centroid replacement 得到“文本结构被擦除”的参考输出。然后用对比解码（contrastive decoding）在生成/选择答案时惩罚那些在“文本被擦除参考”下仍然高概率的候选，从而抑制语言先验驱动的输出，迫使模型更多利用视觉证据。论文还强调了特异性验证：通过 null controls（例如随机/不匹配的替换等）证明增益来自 learned centroid geometry 的破坏而非简单噪声注入；并通过 dose-response sweep（替换强度/比例扫描）展示效果随干预强度单调变化，支持因果解释。\n补充分析：作者做了 segment ablation 与 layer sweep，把竞争定位到特定 token 段（文中指向 answer-option token representations）并观察该“任务分类/敏感性”在不同深度较稳定，暗示问题并非单层偶然现象，而是解码与表征使用方式的系统偏置。","experiments":"论文在 7 个模型、3 类架构家族上做一致性评估（文中未给出模型清单细节片段，但强调跨家族普遍性）。关键数字：\n- 诊断结论：擦除文本质心结构带来的平均准确率损失为 25.9%，擦除视觉质心结构为 6.5%，文本侧代价约为视觉侧的 4×，且这一不对称在多模型上普遍出现。\n- 推理期纠偏：文本质心对比解码在单个视觉感知任务上最高可恢复/提升 +16.9% 准确率；每个模型至少在一个任务上有“有意义”的增益。\n- 训练配方相关性：标准微调模型（SFT、DPO）平均提升 +5.6%，而更复杂的偏好/后训练流水线（SFT+、MPO）平均仅 +1.5%，作者据此提出该干预幅度可作为“残余模态竞争”的训练无关审计指标。\n- 稳健性：在一个被独立工作标记为 visual-prompt fragility 的基准上复现分析（用于证明现象不依赖特定提示脆弱性）。\n（注：你提供的全文片段未包含更细的逐任务/逐模型表格与超参，如 K、替换比例、对比解码公式细节与具体 benchmark 名称列表；若需要我补齐到逐表逐数级别，需要完整 PDF K-means 质心如何构建、在哪个表示层做替换。\n3）读 Section 4.2（null controls + dose-response + segment/layer sweep）：这是论文可信度的关键，决定该方法是否真在测“模态竞争”而非测“对扰动的鲁棒性”。\n4）读 Section 5（与训练配方的关系）：把它当作审计指标的论证，而不是训练指导信号；思考如何在预训练/对齐阶段把该指标变成可优化目标（例如加入跨模态贡献正则、解码时的模态校准、或在 preference data 中显式惩罚无视觉证据的幻觉）。\n预计阅读时间：30–45 分钟可抓住方法与主要结论；若要复现/迁移到你自己的 VLM，需要额外精读实现细节与附录（K、替换位置、对比解码实现）。","authors_note":""},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"Multimodal LMs often fail on tasks that require genuine visual perception because language representations dominate the decision process (modal competition). The paper targets a practical question: can we (i) diagnose how much a model’s predictions rely on text vs. vision with a training-free, forward-pass probe, and (ii) correct the imbalance at inference time without updating weights?","importance":"This is more of a diagnostic + inference-time intervention paper than a new pretraining recipe. Its main value to foundation-model researchers is: (1) a reusable, training-free audit signal for modal dependence based on controlled representation-structure erasure; (2) evidence that text-over-vision dominance is architecture-agnostic across multiple MLM families; (3) a simple two-pass contrastive decoding trick that can recover substantial accuracy on perception-heavy benchmarks, suggesting part of the failure is in how the LM backbone/decoder over-trusts the language manifold. For pretraining, it motivates explicit mechanisms to prevent language priors from overwhelming visual evidence (objective design, representation alignment, and decoding-time calibration).","technical_approach":"$14","experiments":"Reported headline results from the provided full-text excerpt:\n- Universal asymmetry: erasing text centroid structure costs 25.9% accuracy on average vs. 6.5% for vision, i.e., ~4× larger impact for text, across 7 models and 3 architecture families.\n- Inference-time gains: text-centroid contrastive decoding yields up to +16.9% accuracy on individual visual perception tasks; every model improves meaningfully on at least one task.\n- Training-recipe dependence: standard fine-tuned models (SFT, DPO) see larger mean gains (+5.6%) than more advanced post-training pipelines (SFT+, MPO; +1.5%), proposed as a training-free measure of residual modal competition.\n- Robustness: replicated analysis on a benchmark flagged for visual-prompt Dynamics and the Limits of Monitoring Modality Reliance in Vision-Language Models","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p3","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"multimodal","cover_url":"/covers/2604_14888.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL","cs.AI","cs.CV","cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文要回答的核心问题是：在视觉-语言模型（VLM）的链式思维（CoT）推理过程中，模型的“预测/置信度”是否会随中间推理步骤发生实质性修正（而非事后合理化），以及在不同模态占优（文本主导→纯视觉）与模态冲突（误导文本 vs 视觉证据）条件下，模型对模态信息的依赖能否从CoT轨迹中被可靠“监控/识别”（monitorability）。","importance":"对预训练/后训练研究的直接价值在于提供了一套“过程级”诊断框架：不再只看最终准确率，而是用CoT前缀条件下的答案置信度轨迹来刻画推理训练（reasoning-trained）到底带来的是“可纠错的推理过程”还是“更强的自洽与惯性”。这对RL reasoning、VLM对齐、以及多模态数据配比/训练目标设计都有启发：如果模型在早期就锁定答案并在后续CoT中强化（answer inertia），那么增加CoT数据或RL鼓励长推理可能只是在放大路径依赖与不可监控的模态偏置，而非提升基于证据的逐步推断。","technical_approach":"方法上，作者把一次CoT生成切分为多个“推理步骤”（CoT前缀），并在每个前缀条件下评估模型对最终答案选项的置信度（本质是对同一最终答案的条件概率/打分随t变化的轨迹）。围绕该轨迹提出两类分析：\n1) 推理是否纠错：用“净增益/纠错效应（net-gain）”与“截断（truncation）”分析衡量中间步骤对最终正确性的贡献——如果早期错误但后续能翻盘，说明存在纠错；若早期就确定且后续只强化，说明惯性/合理化。\n2) 模态敏感性与可监控性：在MathVerse与PhyX中利用官方/构造的多版本输入（text-dominant、text-lite、vision-intensive、vision-dominant、vision-only等）系统改变文本/视觉信息占比；并通过加入与视觉证据冲突的“误导文本线索”做受控干预，观察模型是否被带偏，以及这种带偏是否会在CoT轨迹中显式体现（即CoT是否暴露其依赖了文本而非图像）。\n模型覆盖18个VLM，分两类训练范式：纯指令微调（Instruct）与显式多步推理/Thinking（含RL产生<think>的Qwen3-VL-Thinking、InternVL3.5 Thinking mode）。核心创新不在提出新训练法，而在提出跨模型、跨模态条件的“推理动态学”测量与对比框架，并把“模态依赖的可监控性”作为新的失败模式来刻画。","experiments":"全文给出的实验设置要点包括：\n- 数据：MathVerse（每种模态变体各436道，多选题）、PhyX（text-dominant 1000、vision-dominant 440、vision-only 1000）、ScienceQA-IMG测试集2017。\n- 模型：Qwen2.5-VL-Instruct(3B/7B/32B)、Qwen3-VL-Instruct(4B/8B/32B)、InternVL3(2B/8B/38B)、InternVL3.5(4B/8B/38B)；推理类含Qwen3-VL-Thinking(4B/8B/32B, RL产CoT)与InternVL3.5 Thinking。\n- 主要发现（定性层面，论文主张）：\n  1) 普遍存在answer inertia：模型往往在CoT早期就对最终答案形成高置信承诺，后续步骤更多是强化而非修正。\n  2) reasoning-trained相对更“可纠错”，但收益强依赖模态条件：从文本主导到纯视觉，纠错/增益模式会显著变化。\n  3) A Teacher-Student Cooperation Framework to Synthesize Student-Consistent SFT Data","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p2","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_14164.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"在“推理型/思维链”模型上做 SFT 时，直接用更强 teacher 生成的合成数据往往不升反降；论文试图定位关键原因之一为 teacher 与 student 的“风格分布”显著不一致，导致 SFT 过程中 style token 的对齐成本干扰了 capability token（解题/代码/数值等）的学习，进而出现性能退化甚至灾难性遗忘。","importance":"对预训练本体不是直接贡献，但对“后训练数据科学/数据分布匹配”非常有启发：1）把合成数据的分布冲突从笼统的 domain shift 细化为 token 级别的 style vs capability 分解；2）提出一种可操作的数据合成协议，让合成数据在能力上继承 teacher、在表述风格上贴近 student，从而降低对 reasoning 模型的 SFT 干扰；3）对持续学习/避免遗忘也有间接价值：通过控制非关键 token 的分布，减少对既有行为模式的破坏。对基座研究员而言，核心启发是“合成数据不只是更强就好，关键是与 student 的生成分布兼容”，尤其在 reasoning 模型（带 thinking/final 双段）上更敏感。","technical_approach":"TESSY（Teacher–Student Cooperation Data Synthesis）的关键是把输出序列 token 划分为两类并进行“交替生成”：\n\n1）Token 分解：定义 capability tokens（与任务求解直接相关，如代码、数值、关键操作符等）集合 T_Cap，与 style tokens（语气、衔接、话语标记等任务无关文本）集合 T_Sty。训练目标可分解为 L_Cap 与 L_Sty；作者论证 reasoning 模型场景下，强行让 student 学 teacher 的 style（优化 L_Sty）会变难并反过来伤害 L_Cap 的学习。\n\n2）合成目标：希望合成数据满足——capability token 分布来自 teacher，style token 分布尽量贴近 student。\n\n3）交替生成机制：用 teacher 负责生成“解题相关片段/关键 token”，student 负责生成“风格/连接性 token”。为实现细粒度控制，提出 generate-then-rollback：先生成一段，再根据判别/规则决定哪些 token 应由另一方接管并回滚到某个位置继续生成，从而在同一条序列内实现 teacher/student 的分工。\n\n4）适配 reasoning 模型形态：论文动机来自 reasoning 模型输出常包含 thinking 与 final 两段，且不同模型的叙述方式差异更大；TESSY 试图在保留 teacher 推理质量的同时，让表述更像 student 以减少分布冲突。\n\n从方法本质看，这是“数据合成时的 on-policy 风格约束/混合采样”，而不是训练时的 loss reweighting；它把分布匹配前移到数据生成阶段。","experiments":"论文在引言给出了关键结果（代码推理任务）：\n- 设 teacher 为 GPT-OSS-120B、student 为 Qwen3-8B。直接用 teacher-only 合成数据做 SFT 会导致 student 性能下降：LiveCodeBench-Pro 最高下降 3.25%，OJBench 最高下降 10.02%。\n- 使用 TESSY 合成数据进行 SFT，则在相同基准上提升 Qwen3-8B：LiveCodeBench-Pro +11.25%，OJBench +6.68%。\n- 还报告了跨 teacher 的一致性：可与 DeepSeek-R1、以及“student 相关”的 Qwen3-235B-A22B-Thinking 等 teacher 搭配仍有收益。\n\n你提供的全文片段尚未包含：合成数据规模、cap/style 判定规则或模型、rollback 触发策略、SFT 超参、以及更完整的消融（仅 teacher、仅 student、交替频率、cap/style 划分噪声敏感性等）。这些细节决定方法可复现性与可迁移性。","reading_guide":"泛读建议（约 30–45 分钟）：\n1）先读 Approach 中对 L_Cap/L_Sty 的形式化与“style 干扰 capability 学习”的论证，这是本文的核心假设。\n2）重点看 generate-then-rollback 的具体算法流程（若后文有伪代码/图 2），弄清：cap/style 如何识别、何时切换 teacher/student、回滚窗口多大、额外采样开销。\n3）看实验部分的对比与消融：尤其是 teacher-only 退化的条件（哪些任务/哪些 teacher-student 组合最严重），以及 TESSY 的收益是否来自“更像 student 的表述”还是“更少遗忘”。","authors_note":""},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"SFT on emerging reasoning models can degrade performance when using synthetic data generated purely by a stronger teacher. The paper attributes a major cause to stylistic distribution mismatch between teacher and student: forcing the student to imitate teacher-specific style tokens interferes with learning task-critical capability tokens, leading to drops and potential forgetting.","importance":"Not a pretraining-method paper, but highly relevant to post-training data science for foundation models. Key takeaway: synthetic data quality is not monotonic in teacher strength; compatibility with the student’s output distribution (especially style/format for reasoning models with thinking/final structure) can dominate. The token-level decomposition into capability vs style provides a concrete lens for diagnosing distribution conflict, and the proposed synthesis protocol is an actionable way to reduce SFT-induced regression—also conceptually aligned with continual-learning goals (minimize unnecessary distributional drift).","technical_approach":"$15","experiments":"Key reported numbers (from the provided Optimization","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p2","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_14214.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL","cs.AI"],"summary":{"core_problem":"自动化提示词优化（APO）在复杂推理任务上往往只优化准确率，导致系统提示词和模型输出推理过程越来越冗长，推理 token 成本/时延急剧上升；论文要解决的是：在不显著牺牲推理正确率的前提下，把“输出长度/成本”作为一等公民纳入提示词搜索目标，得到能诱导模型生成更短、更“只含关键信息”的推理与答案的提示词。","importance":"对基座预训练本身不是直接贡献（更偏后训练/推理侧的prompting与系统优化），但对“推理token经济学”很有启发：它把长度惩罚做成可被APO利用的“文本梯度/反馈信号”，提供了一种在不改模型权重的情况下压缩推理轨迹的工程化路径。对预训练研究的间接价值在于：提示了未来在预训练或RL pretrain阶段可以显式引入“token成本/长度”正则（类似compute-aware或budget-aware目标），以及评估时不应只看accuracy，还要看accuracy-per-token。","technical_approach":"论文提出 CROP（Cost-Regularized Optimization of Prompts），核心思想是在APO的反馈回路里加入“输出长度正则”。其框架沿用“LLM作为元优化器”的提示词迭代：给定当前系统prompt p、输入x、目标模型M生成输出ŷ，然后由评估器产生反馈用于改写p。与只给准确率反馈不同，CROP额外构造一个与token长度相关的惩罚反馈：当输出超过某个最小阈值时，对超出的长度施加惩罚，并把该惩罚以自然语言/文本反馈的形式与任务反馈进行聚合（文中称 textual summation / continuous length-penalty gradient）。直观上，它逼迫元优化器在prompt里写入更强的“简洁约束”和“只输出关键推理”的指令，从而改变目标模型的输出分布（更短、更符号化）。论文还强调该机制会诱导出类似人工设计的压缩推理风格（如Chain-of-Draft/符号化草稿），但由优化过程自动发现。需要注意：从全文给出的描述看，它更像一种“可微/连续”的长度反馈设计理念，但实现上仍是通过文本化反馈驱动的离散prompt搜索，而非对模型参数做真正梯度更新。","experiments":"在 80.6%。全文片段未给出更细的实验表格细节（如具体使用的目标模型、prompt迭代轮数、长度阈值设定、各数据集分别的accuracy与token均值/分位数、与其他APO基线的对比数字、以及是否统计端到端延迟），因此无法在此补充更精确的参数量/数据规模/逐项提升幅度。就论文叙述而言，关键现象是输出长度分布被显著左移，并出现“更压缩的符号推理结构”的涌现。","reading_guide":"泛读建议：重点看 Methodology 中长度正则如何被形式化（长度阈值、惩罚如何转成文本反馈、与任务反馈如何聚合）、以及实验部分关于“token分布变化/效率-准确率权衡”的图表（通常是accuracy vs tokens或长度直方图/箱线图）。如果你关心预训练/RL pretrain启发，建议带着两个问题读：1）这种长度正则是否会诱导捷径/不可靠的隐式推理（accuracy不变但鲁棒性下降）？2）该正则能否迁移为训练目标（例如在RL阶段把token成本作为reward penalty）以及与“隐藏推理/只输出答案”策略的关系。预计阅读时间：20–30分钟抓主线，若要复现/迁移到训练目标需更细读反馈构造与超参。","authors_note":""},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"Automatic prompt optimization (APO) for reasoning tasks typically optimizes accuracy only, which tends to bloat both the system prompt and the model’s generated reasoning traces, causing large latency and token costs. The paper targets the problem of making APO explicitly cost-aware: optimize prompts that preserve reasoning accuracy while aggressively reducing output length/tokens.","importance":"Not a pretraining contribution per se (it sits closer to prompting/inference-time optimization), but it is relevant to foundation-model research through the lens of “accuracy-per-token” and budget-aware objectives. It operationalizes a length/token regularizer inside the prompt-search loop, suggesting a broader direction: incorporate token-cost regularization into RL pretraining or post-training, and evaluate reasoning systems with cost-sensitive metrics rather than accuracy alone.","technical_approach":"CROP (Cost-Regularized Optimization of Prompts) augments APO with an explicit output-length regularization signal. In the standard loop, a meta-optimizer LLM iteratively rewrites the system prompt based on feedback from running a target model on inputs. CROP adds a length penalty when the generated output exceeds a minimal threshold, and injects this penalty as textual feedback alongside the usual task-accuracy feedback (the paper frames this as a continuous length-penalty “gradient” aggregated via textual summation). The meta-optimizer is thus pushed to discover prompts that instruct the target model to produce concise, information-dense reasoning—often yielding compressed, symbolic “draft-like” reasoning styles without manual prompt engineering. Conceptually, it’s a multi-objective prompt search where token count is treated as a first-class constraint.","experiments":"Evaluated on GSM8K, LogiQA, and BIG-Bench Hard. The headline result is up to an 80.6% reduction in token consumption while maintaining competitive accuracy relative to unconstrained Chain-of-Thought prompting. The provided full-text excerpt does not include the detailed tables (model identities/sizes, per-dataset accuracy and average tokens, variance, number of optimization steps, or baseline APO comparisons), so more granular numeric reporting cannot be verified here beyond the stated aggregate reduction.","reading_guide":"Skim the Methodology for (i) how the length threshold and penalty are defined, (ii) how the penalty is converted into textual feedback, and (iii) how it is combined with task feedback in the prompt-update loop. In Experiments, focus on plots/tables showing the accuracy–token trade-off and the shift in output-length distributions, plus qualitative examples of the emergent compressed reasoning format. Time: ~20–30 minutes for the main idea; longer if you want to adapt the regularizer into RL-style training objectives.","authors_note":""},"recommendation":{"zh":"别把它当“推理新算法”，而是看它如何把token成本写进优化目标；只读目标函数/正则项与消融就够。","en":"Don’t read it as a new reasoning algorithm—read how they bake token cost into the LLM unlearning 多依赖改权重（parametric unlearning），在持续更新下会累积灾难性遗忘、且处理耗时导致敏感信息在窗口期继续暴露。论文要解决的是：如何在不改动 LLM 权重的前提下，实现可持续、实时、连续到来的遗忘请求处理，同时最大化保留原有知识与效用。","importance":"对基座预训练研究的直接关联偏弱（更偏部署安全/合规与后训练治理），但对“持续学习/持续遗忘”的系统视角有启发：它把 unlearning 从‘擦除参数中的知识’扩展为‘行为层面的拒答/抑制’，并强调 continual setting 下的累积效应与时延约束。作为研究启发点：1）在无法重训/难以精确擦除参数记忆时，行为门控（gating）可能是更可控的工程解；2）把遗忘检测问题转化为高精度检索/判别（embedding + hard negatives）是可扩展路线；3）也暴露了一个研究缺口：行为遗忘并不等价于真正的知识移除，如何定义更强的评测与攻击模型（绕过、提示注入、语义漂移）对预训练与对齐都很关键。","technical_approach":"CURaTE 将方法分为部署前与部署后两阶段：\n- 部署前：训练一个“unlearning sentence embedding model”。训练数据为合成构造，并包含 hard negatives，使得嵌入空间能对‘与遗忘集合相关的查询’与‘无关查询’形成尖锐决策边界（核心是提升对释义/改写的鲁棒匹配与低误拒）。\n- 部署后（实时）：系统持续接收 forget requests，把这些请求的 embedding 追加进数据库；对每个用户 query 计算 embedding，与库中 forget embeddings 做相似度检索/匹配；若相似度超过阈值（或满足判别规则），则触发拒答/不输出，从而实现“behavioral unlearning”。\n关键设计选择：完全不更新 LLM 权重，因此避免 continual parametric updates 带来的灾难性遗忘；同时 embedder 在部署后无需再训练，也不需要 retain/forget 集合参与后续训练，从而把每次新增遗忘请求的成本降到近似常数（主要是向量入库与一次检索）。论文还形式化了 gold standard：理想模型 G* 等价于在 Dr（去除 Df 后的数据）上从头训练得到的模型，用于定义遗忘与保留的评测目标。","experiments":"你提供的全文片段主要覆盖引言与任务形式化，未包含具体基准名称、模型规模、连续遗忘步数、遗忘成功率/误拒率、与 SOTA arrive sequentially and must take effect immediately. Most existing LLM unlearning methods rely on weight updates, which (i) accumulate catastrophic forgetting in the continual setting and (ii) are too slow, leaving a window where sensitive content can still be produced. The paper asks: how can we support real-time continual unlearning while preserving the model’s general utility?","importance":"Relevance to core pretraining is indirect (more governance/safety), but it offers a useful framing for continual unlearning: shift from ‘erasing parametric knowledge’ to ‘behavioral unlearning’ via fast gating. It highlights two constraints often ignored in research prototypes—latency and accumulation over time. It also surfaces an open research gap: behavioral refusal is not true knowledge removal, so stronger evaluation and adversarial threat models (paraphrase, prompt injection, semantic drift) are essential for foundation-model training and alignment.","technical_approach":"CURaTE is a two-stage system.\n- Pre-deployment: train an unlearning sentence-embedding model on a synthetic dataset with hard negatives to create sharp decision boundaries between queries related to the forget set and unrelated queries.\n- Post-deployment (real time): maintain a database of embeddings for incoming forget requests. For each user query, compute its embedding and perform similarity matching against the forget-embedding database; if matched, refuse to answer. The LLM weights are never modified, avoiding catastrophic forgetting from continual parameter updates. The embedder also requires no post-deployment training and does not need retain/forget sets for further optimization, making per-request updates essentially “append + retrieve”.\nThe paper formalizes the gold standard as an ideal model trained from scratch on the retain-only data Dr (excluding Df), using this to define forget/retain evaluation goals.","experiments":"The provided excerpt does not include the experimental section (benchmarks, model sizes, number of continual steps, quantitative forget/retain metrics, latency, or comparisons to SOTA parametric unlearning). LLM Unlearning as an Asymmetric Two-Task Learning Problem","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p2","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_14808.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"LLM 机器遗忘（unlearning）中“忘得干净”和“能力不掉”存在强冲突：仅对 forget set 做梯度上升容易过度遗忘并破坏通用能力；加入 retain set 的梯度下降又会与遗忘梯度相互抵消、训练不稳定。本文核心问题是：如何在存在梯度冲突时，把“保留能力（retention）”作为主目标、把“遗忘（forgetting）”作为辅目标，构造一种可插拔的梯度合成机制，在不牺牲遗忘效果的前提下显著提升保留性能。","importance":"对持续学习/遗忘方向的直接贡献是把 unlearning 明确建模为“不对称两任务学习”，并给出“保留优先”的梯度合成范式：这比以往把 retain/forget 当作对称多目标或简单加权更贴近真实需求（部署时 retention 往往是硬约束）。方法层面把多任务冲突优化（PCGrad）系统性迁移到 unlearning，并提出更强约束的 SAGO，使更新方向与 retain 梯度保持非负对齐甚至更强的逐元素符号一致，从而在安全遗忘任务上提供一种通用的、与具体 unlearning loss 解耦的优化组件。对预训练研究的启发在于：当我们做持续学习/数据删除/安全擦除时，可以把“主任务能力守恒”写成几何约束（梯度对齐/符号约束），用优化层的结构性约束替代经验性权重调参。","technical_approach":"论文提出一个两阶段的“保留优先梯度合成（retention-prioritized gradient synthesis）”框架：\n1) 梯度抽取解耦：分别从 retain 目标得到 g_r（通常是对 retain set 的 GD），从 forget 目标得到 g_f（可能来自 GA、NPO、SimNPO 等遗忘目标），不在 loss 层面直接线性加和。\n2) 冲突感知合成：构造最终更新梯度 g，使其与 g_r 的夹角满足保留优先约束。\n\n具体实例化两种合成器：\n- PCGrad 适配版：借鉴多任务 PCGrad 的“投影去冲突”思想，当 g_f 与 g_r 冲突（内积为负）时，将 g_f 在 g_r 的反向分量投影去除，得到与 g_r 非负对齐的遗忘分量，再与 g_r 组合更新。关键点是把 retain 作为锚点（primary），遗忘梯度只允许在不伤害 retain 的可行锥内起作用。\n- SAGO（Sign-Aligned Gradient Optimization / 或类似命名，文中核心是 sign-constrained synthesis）：在保证 cos(g, g_r) ≥ 0 的基础上进一步收紧对齐：对合成梯度施加逐元素符号约束，使 g 的每一维更新方向与 g_r 的符号一致（或至少不相反），从而避免“整体夹角不冲突但局部维度破坏 retain”的情况。论文给出理论性质：PCGrad 与 SAGO 都能保证与 g_r 非负余弦相似度；SAGO 通过构造性的符号约束实现更严格（更紧）的对齐界。\n\n框架的可插拔性：作者强调该合成器可叠加在 GA+GD、NPO+GD、SimNPO+GD 等不同遗忘目标之上，属于优化层组件而非新 loss；这点对后续扩展到其他遗忘/持续学习目标很关键。","experiments":"实验覆盖两个主流 LLM unlearning 基准：WMDP（含 Bio/Cyber 等子域）与 RWKU。核心结论是：在“遗忘效果相当（comparable forgetting）”的前提下，SAGO 显著提升 retention。\n- WMDP：相对 naive 方法（未做冲突处理的基线），在 MMLU 上 Bio 子域提升 17.8–30.7 分、Cyber 子域提升 4.1–11.7 分；在与 PCGrad 对比时，SAGO 仍额外提升约 0.4–1.2 分，同时保持相当或更好的遗忘效果。\n- RWKU：同样观察到 retention 的一致提升（文中描述为“similar improvements”，具体数值需结合正文表格/附录）。\n论文还强调了“冲突仍然存在”这一现象：即便 NPO/SimNPO 通过有界化与平滑缓解 GA 崩塌，retain/forget 梯度冲突仍会导致能力损失；合成器能系统性解决这一点。消融方面（从全文结构推断）通常会包含：不同遗忘目标 + 是否使用 PCGrad/SAGO、不同层/不同数据配比下的 retention/forgetting 曲线对比，以及余弦相似度/冲突比例等诊断指标（建议读者在正文图表中核对）。","reading_guide":"泛读建议（约 25–35 分钟）：\n- 先看 Introduction 中对“对称权衡不符合需求”的动机，以及 Figure 1（a)(b)(c) 的直观对比，理解为何要把 retention 设为 primary。\n- 精看 Method/Framework：重点抓住“梯度抽取解耦 + 冲突感知合成”的两阶段结构，以及 PCGrad 适配与 SAGO 的差异（尤其是 SAGO 的逐元素符号约束如何构造、是否会削弱遗忘强度）。\n- 看理论部分的两个保证：cosine 非负对齐与 SAGO 更紧对齐界，理解它们对应的优化可行域。\n- 看 WMDP 的主表/主图：对齐“comparable forgetting”条件下 retention 的提升幅度；再对照 PCGrad vs SAGO 的增益是否稳定。\n值得深挖点：SAGO 的符号约束在高维参数空间是否过强、是否会导致遗忘不足；以及当 retain 梯度噪声较大/小 batch 时，符号约束是否更稳健或更脆弱（这与预训练/持续学习中的梯度噪声尺度直接相关）。","authors_note":"SUSTech-NLP（代码仓库为 sustech-nlp/SAGO）；其余作者与机构在给定全文片段中无法完全确认。"},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"LLM unlearning suffers from a persistent retain–forget trade-off: pure gradient ascent on the forget set often causes over-forgetting and broad capability degradation, while adding retain-set gradient descent introduces strong gradient conflicts that destabilize training and still harms utility. The paper’s core question is how to enforce retention as the primary objective and treat forgetting as an auxiliary objective via a principled gradient synthesis rule that resolves conflicts while keeping forgetting effectiveness.","importance":"The key contribution is a reframing of unlearning as an asymmetric two-task learning problem (retention-primary, forgetting-auxiliary) and a plug-and-play optimization-layer solution: retention-prioritized gradient synthesis. This is impactful for continual learning / data deletion settings because it replaces ad-hoc loss weighting with geometric constraints on update directions (alignment with retain gradients). Methodologically, it ports PCGrad-style conflict resolution into unlearning and proposes a stronger sign-constrained synthesizer (SAGO), offering a general component that can sit on top of multiple unlearning objectives (GA, NPO, SimNPO + retain GD).","technical_approach":"$16","experiments":"Evaluations are conducted on WMDP and RWKU unlearning benchmarks. baseline; SAGO further adds ~0.4–1.2 points over the PCGrad variant while maintaining comparable or better forgetting effectiveness.\n- Similar retention gains are reported on RWKU (the provided full-text excerpt does not include the exact table values).\nThe experimental narrative also supports the motivation: even bounded/smoothed unlearning objectives (NPO/SimNPO) do not eliminate retain–forget gradient conflicts; conflict-aware synthesis is the missing piece.","reading_guide":"Skim plan (~25–35 minutes):\n- Read the Introduction + Figure 1 to internalize the asymmetric framing constraint is constructed and how it trades off forgetting strength.\n- Check the theoretical propositions guaranteeing non-negative cosine similarity and the “tighter alignment” claim for SAGO.\n- retain gradients (small batches / domain shift), and whether the constraint can undercut forgetting when the optimal forget direction genuinely requires moving against some retain Reasoning","abstract":"","starred":false,"priority":"p2","reading_tier":"skim","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_15148.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.AI","cs.CL","cs.IR"],"summary":{"core_problem":"在“边思考边检索”的RL后训练（search-augmented reasoning）中，现有GRPO/trajectory-level奖励无法对同一轨迹内不同检索步骤的query质量进行细粒度归因，并且在所有采样轨迹都答错时优势函数近零导致梯度信号塌缩。论文要解决的是：如何构造一个不依赖额外标注/奖励模型、能在失败轨迹中仍提供学习信号的step-level检索奖励，从而更有效地学习检索query生成策略。","importance":"对预训练主线是间接贡献（属于post-training/RL范式），但对“RL pretrain/持续学习式工具使用”很有启发：它把检索步骤的信用分配从episode级别下沉到step级别，并用反事实（random docs）构造可计算的过程奖励，缓解早期训练的全失败零梯度问题。方法本质上是把‘检索是否带来信息增益’形式化为可微的训练信号，可能迁移到更广的tool-use（代码执行、数据库查询、网页浏览）场景，作为通用的process reward设计模板。","technical_approach":"IG-Search的核心是“信息增益（IG）step reward”。对每一次search step：\n- 固定检索器，模型生成一个检索query并取回文档D_real；同时构造一个反事实基线D_rand（随机文档）。\n- 用模型对gold answer的置信度提升来度量该检索的有效性：比较在条件化D_real vs D_rand时，模型对正确答案的log-prob/置信度差异，作为该step的IG奖励。直觉是：好的检索query应当检索到能显著提高模型对正确答案概率的证据文档。\n- 训练上仍基于GRPO，但引入per-token advantage modulation：把step-level IG信号回传到对应的query token，使同一轨迹内不同检索步骤获得不同强度的梯度，而不是共享一个trajectory advantage。\n- 稳定化机制（§2.4）：用于防止退化行为（例如通过某些投机方式提高“对gold的置信度”但不真正改进检索质量，或IG尺度不稳导致训练发散）。从引言描述看，IG-Search的优势在于：不需要turn级标注（如子问题）、不需要单独训练reward model，仅用标准QA对即可计算检索过程奖励。","experiments":"任务覆盖7个QA基准：单跳（NQ、TriviaQA、PopQA）与多跳（HotpotQA、2WikiMultihopQA、Musique、Bamboogle）。\n- Base model：Qwen2.5-3B上，IG-Search平均EM=0.430；相对最强trajectory-level基线MR-Search提升+1.6 EM；相对step-level方法GiGPO提升+0.9 EM；并强调多跳任务增益更明显。\n- 规模泛化：在Qwen2.5-7B上也在所有基准上稳定提升（引言未给出逐项数字）。\n- 论文还声称其step-level信号在“all-failure”场景仍非零，从而改善早期训练；建议在正文实验/消融中重点核对：IG reward与最终EM的相关性、random-doc baseline的选择对方差/偏差的影响、以及advantage modulation对不同step的梯度分配是否真的提升了query质量（例如检索命中率/证据覆盖率）。\n（你提供的全文片段未包含完整实验表与消融细节；若补充对应章节，我可以进一步抽取每个数据集的EM、训练步数/采样轨迹数、检索次数上限、以及稳定化技巧带来的定量收益。）","reading_guide":"泛读建议（45–60分钟）：\n- 先读§2方法定义：IG如何计算（尤其是“置信度/对数概率”具体形式、对gold answer的token级聚合方式、以及random docs反事实基线如何采样）。\n- 再读§2.3的per-token advantage modulation：这是把step reward真正“对齐到query token”的关键实现细节。\n- 必读§2.4稳定化：这类过程奖励很容易被hack，稳定化细节往往决定能否复现。\n- 实验部分优先看：多跳数据集上的提升、all-failure场景的训练曲线、以及对比IGPO/StepSearch/GiGPO/MR-Search的差异分析。\n- 值得深挖：把IG视为一种“检索器固定时的可学习query质量度量”，思考能否扩展到可训练检索器（joint training）或更一般的tool调用（以反事实工具输出为baseline）。","authors_note":""},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"In RL training for search-augmented reasoning, trajectory-level rewards (e.g., GRPO-style) fail to assign credit to individual search queries within a rollout and collapse to near-zero learning signal when all sampled trajectories are incorrect. The paper addresses how to design a step-level reward that directly evaluates query quality, requires no extra annotations or separate reward model, and remains informative even in all-failure regimes.","importance":"Primarily a post-training/RL contribution, but conceptually relevant to RL-pretrain and continual tool-use learning: it operationalizes a retrieval-grounded process reward via counterfactual comparison, improving credit assignment and mitigating early-training zero-gradient issues. The broader takeaway is a reusable template for tool-use rewards: measure the marginal information contributed by a tool call relative to a randomized baseline.","technical_approach":"IG-Search introduces an Information Gain (IG) reward per search step:\n- For each generated search query, retrieve documents D_real with a fixed retriever; construct a counterfactual baseline D_rand using random documents.\n- Define the step reward as how much conditioning on D_real increases the model’s confidence (log-probability) of the gold answer compared to conditioning on D_rand.\n- Integrate this into GRPO via per-token advantage modulation so that tokens responsible for different search steps receive gradients proportional to their step-level IG, rather than sharing a single trajectory advantage.\n- Add stabilization mechanisms (Section 2.4) to prevent degenerate optimization and control reward scale/variance.\nKey differentiator vs prior step-level signals (e.g., IGPO): the reward is explicitly retrieval-grounded and counterfactual, aiming to isolate query quality from other within-turn effects.","experiments":"Benchmarks: 7 QA datasets—single-hop (NQ, TriviaQA, PopQA) and step-level baseline GiGPO by +0.9 EM on average; gains are reported to be larger on multi-hop tasks.\n- With Qwen2.5-7B, improvements are consistent across all benchmarks (per-dataset numbers not natural-language explanations produced by LLMs can be persuasive yet epistemically unfaithful—i.e., they may not reflect the internal evidence that actually drove the model’s decision. The paper addresses (1) how to evaluate epistemic faithfulness with a practical causal/counterfactual protocol, and (2) how to improve faithfulness without training by grounding explanations in attribution signals.","importance":"Indirectly relevant to foundation-model pretraining: it strengthens the message that CoT/rationales are not inherently faithful, and it introduces a more causal evaluation setup plus a lightweight inference-time intervention. For pretraining/continual learning researchers, it motivates incorporating evidence–explanation consistency as an explicit objective/regularizer if auditability is a goal, and it provides a concrete measurement tool to diagnose faithfulness gaps.","technical_approach":"The evaluation protocol uses counterfactual hint interventions. The model first answers a question normally (a0). Then it is re-queried with a crafted hint intended to flip the answer (covering multiple hint types such as authority cues, metadata wrappers, sycophancy-like suggestions, and unethical-information cues). If the answer flips, the hint is treated as a verified causal driver; the model is then asked to justify the new answer, and explanations that incorporate the hint-consistent evidence are deemed more epistemically faithful. To mitigate unfaithfulness, the paper proposes Faithfulness Serum: compute token-level attributions with PE-LRP for the prompt/answer, then inject the attribution heatmap into the model via the attention mechanism during explanation generation. A dose parameter α controls the strength—too low has little effect; too high harms fluency—so one selects the largest α that preserves intelligibility.","experiments":"The paper reports that both open- and closed-source models are largely epistemically unfaithful under the proposed benchmark, and that Faithfulness Serum improves faithfulness in a dose-dependent manner. From a pretraining perspective, consider failure modes (models learning to parrot hints) and how attribution–explanation alignment could be turned into a training-time constraint. LLM 进行“流式（streaming）有害意图探测”需要在生成过程中基于前缀实时判别，但现有基于表示的 probe 往往被少数高分 token/窗口主导：当 CBRN 术语出现在良性语境（科普/学术讨论）中时会产生大量误报。本文要解决的核心问题是：在只给 exchange-level 标签、推理却要 token-level 流式输出的设定下，如何设计更鲁棒的聚合目标，让判别依赖跨片段的一致证据而非孤立尖峰，从而显著降低低 FPR 区间的错误。","importance":"这不是预训练方法论文，但对“安全相关持续监控/对齐后部署”有方法论启发：很多安全探测失败并非数据不够，而是训练目标（聚合方式）诱导了 shortcut learning（关键词尖峰）。本文把改进点放在 streaming 聚合目标与正则上，提供了一个轻量、可插拔的 probe 训练范式：Top-K 支持窗口聚合 + 片段方差正则，专门优化低误报区间（1% FPR）表现。对基座研究的间接价值在于：当我们做预训练/后训练的安全信号建模或表征探测时，目标函数的“证据分布形态”约束（鼓励分布式一致证据）可能比继续堆数据更关键。","technical_approach":"方法建立在滑动窗口聚合的 streaming probe 框架上：冻结目标 LLM，从每个 token、每层抽取内部激活作为特征，训练线性 probe 输出 token-level logit z_t，并通过因果滑窗（例如最近 M=16）做平滑得到更稳定的流式信号。关键创新在于把“如何从一串 token-level logit 得到 exchange-level 判别”从 softmax/hardmax 这类尖峰敏感聚合，改为更保守的多证据聚合，并加入抑制尖峰的正则：\n1) Top-K supportive-window pooling：不再让单个最高分窗口决定结果，而是要求多个窗口共同提供支持（取 Top-K 窗口的聚合），从目标上迫使模型学习跨片段一致的有害证据。\n2) Segment Variance Regularization (SegVar)：对选中的证据窗口的 logit 幅度离散度施加惩罚，抑制“单窗口尖峰、其余窗口很低”的模式；并且该正则选择性地施加在 benign 交换上，因为误报主要来自良性语境中的关键词尖峰。\n此外，作者系统比较 probe 的特征来源：Attention/MLP 输出在其实验中比常用 residual stream 更强更稳。并分析对抗性混淆（字符级 cipher 微调）下的可迁移性：在 base model 上训练的 probe baseline（AUROC=97.40%）上，进一步将“剩余错误边际”降低 31.2%（作者用 error margin 口径表述）。\n- logspace-AUROC（强调低 FPR 区间）提升 16.80%。\n- 对抗性混淆迁移：在字符级 cipher 微调场景下，probe 仍可迁移，最高 AUROC 达到 98.85%。\n设计分析结论：Attention/MLP 激活作为 probe 输入优于 residual stream（具体提升幅度需结合正文/附录表格）。","reading_guide":"泛读建议（约 30–45 分钟）：\n- 先看 Introduction + Figure 1（若有）理解“良性语境含敏感词导致尖峰误报”的失败模式，以及为何说问题不只是数据。\n- 精看 Method：Top-K supportive-window pooling prefix-only decisions during generation, but existing representation-based probes often over-weight a few high-scoring tokens/windows. In CBRN domains, benign expert discussions contain the same terminology as harmful requests, so spike-driven aggregation yields false alarms. The paper addresses how to redesign the streaming aggregation objective so predictions require consistent evidence across multiple segments rather than isolated keyword spikes, improving performance in the low-FPR regime.","importance":"While not a pretraining paper, it offers a useful lesson for safety monitoring and probing: failures can be objective-induced shortcut learning, not merely data scarcity. vs RL）、推理时策略”三类因素，回答：LLM 是否能在可组合的序列优化问题（SOP）上实现系统性泛化，并区分两种 OOD：未见地图的空间迁移 vs 更长规划长度的长度扩展。","importance":"对预训练/数据科学的价值在于：1）给出一个高度可控的“可组合规划”测试床，把常见的泛化争论从自然语料的混杂因素中剥离出来；2）明确指出长度扩展失败的主要机制是递归不稳定（recursive instability），即局部决策误差在长链条组合中放大；3）数据配比结论更贴近预训练直觉：在固定预算下，“更多不同问题（start-end 对）”比“同一问题更多解/轨迹”更利于迁移泛化；覆盖更广的原子技能（primitives coverage）比更复杂的组合多样性更关键；4）RL 在该类任务上更多是稳定训练、未突破 SFT 上限，且可能收缩有效解空间——对 RL pretrain / RLVR 的能力边界与副作用提供了负面证据。整体属于机制+数据/训练范式分析，对 scaling/数据课程设计有启发。","technical_approach":"1）问题形式化：将最短路视为可组合 SOP，强调最优子结构（Opt(i,j)=Opt(i,k)∘Opt(k,j)）。\n2）两条泛化轴：\n- 空间迁移（spatial transfer）：测试在完全未见过的地图 G 上，模型是否能把学到的移动规则 f(i,j|G) 迁移过去。\n- 长度扩展（length scaling）：在同一地图内测试更长规划视野/更长路径的 start-end 对，检验能否把短程解递归组合成长程解。\n3）评测设置：direct-answer，要求一次性生成完整路径，不提供中间推理步骤（避免把 CoT 当作额外监督信道）。\n4）可控变量：系统改变训练数据构成（问题数 vs 解数、primitive 覆盖 vs 组合多样性、训练样本最大长度等）、训练范式（SFT 与可验证奖励下的 RL）、以及推理时策略（inference-time scaling/advanced decoding）。\n5）失败模式分析：通过结构化环境可视化错误，提出长度扩展失败源于递归不稳定：模型在长链条上无法维持一致的局部最优决策，导致早期小错在后续状态中累积放大。","experiments":"论文在引言中汇总的关键结论（具体数值需看正文表格）：\n1）空间迁移强：模型能在未见地图上保持较好表现，支持一定程度的系统性结构泛化。\n2）长度扩展弱：在更长规划长度上持续失败，且归因于 recursive instability。\n3）数据因素：固定训练预算下，把预算用在“更多不同问题（distinct questions）”优于“同一问题更多解（more solutions）”；选择 primitive 覆盖更广的问题比增加 primitive 组合多样性更有效。长度扩展则需要训练集中包含“略长于测试目标的样本”或至少覆盖更长例子。\n4）训练范式：RL 主要提升稳定性但不超过 SFT 的性能天花板，错误模式相似；即使用更强推理策略，RL 仍低于最佳 SFT，并呈现限制有效解空间的迹象。\n5）推理策略：先进推理时方法能提升 SFT/RL 的总体表现，但无法挽救长度扩展失败。","reading_guide":"建议泛读（45–60分钟）：\n- 先读实验设置/数据生成：两条 OOD 轴如何严格构造（未见地图 vs 更长长度），以及 direct-answer 输出格式与判分规则。\n- 重点读“长度扩展失败”章节：作者如何定义与诊断 recursive instability（最好配合错误可视化/案例）。\n- 再读数据消融：distinct questions vs solutions、primitive coverage vs combination diversity，这部分对预训练数据配比/课程学习最有迁移价值。\n- 最后读 SFT vs RL 与 inference-time scaling：关注 RL 为何不超越 SFT、以及“限制解空间”的证据链（奖励设计、探索、输出分布变化等）。","authors_note":""},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"Using a tightly controlled synthetic shortest-path environment, disentangle how training data, training paradigm (SFT vs RL), and inference-time strategies affect systematic generalization in composable sequential optimization problems—separating spatial transfer to unseen maps from length scaling to longer-horizon planning.","importance":"For pretraining/data/scaling researchers, the paper’s value is methodological and diagnostic: it provides a clean testbed where OOD axes are unambiguous, and shows a consistent asymmetry—strong spatial transfer but persistent length-scaling failure driven by recursive instability (small local errors amplify when recursively composing decisions). It also yields actionable data-design insights: under a fixed budget, more distinct questions (start–goal pairs) beats more solutions per question; broader primitive coverage matters more than richer primitive combinations. Finally, it offers a cautionary result for RL(-style) training: RL stabilizes but does not exceed the best SFT ceiling and may shrink the effective solution space, even with stronger decoding—relevant to RL pretrain/RLVR expectations.","technical_approach":"Formalization: cast shortest-path planning as a composable SOP with optimal substructure, enabling a principled notion of “systematic generalization” as rule application beyond training support.\nOOD axes: (1) spatial transfer—evaluate on entirely unseen maps; (2) length scaling—evaluate longer-horizon start–goal pairs within the same map.\nEvaluation protocol: direct-answer generation of the full path (no intermediate reasoning), reducing confounds from CoT-style supervision.\nFactorized pipeline study: independently vary (i) training data properties (question vs solution allocation, primitive coverage, max training length), (ii) training paradigm (SFT vs RL with verifiable rewards), and (iii) inference-time strategies (advanced decoding/inference-time scaling).\nAnalysis: characterize failure modes via the structured environment and attribute length-scaling breakdown to recursive instability.","experiments":"Key reported findings (see main tables/figures for exact numbers):\n- Spatial transfer is strong: models generalize to unseen maps reasonably well.\n- Length scaling consistently fails: performance drops on longer-horizon problems, explained by recursive instability.\n- Data ablations: allocating budget to more distinct questions improves transfer; selecting questions with broader primitive coverage helps more than increasing primitive-combination diversity. Length scaling requires exposure to slightly longer training examples.\n- SFT vs RL: RL improves stability but does not beat SFT’s best performance; error patterns are similar.\n- Inference-time strategies: stronger decoding helps overall but cannot rescue length-scaling failures; RL remains below best SFT even with these strategies and appears to restrict the solution space.","reading_guide":"Skim (45–60 min):\n1) Experimental setup: how maps are generated, how train/test supports are separated, and how spatial-transfer vs length-scaling splits are constructed.\n2)
